-   // History Panel
  historyPanelOpen: false,
  historyPanelWidth: (() => {
    try {
      const saved = localStorage.getItem('noted-terminal-history-panel-width');
      return saved ? Math.max(280, Math.min(700, parseInt(saved, 10))) : 580;
    } catch { return 580; }
  })(),
  historyScrollToUuid: null,
  setHistoryPanelOpen: (open) => set({ historyPanelOpen: open }),

+   // History Panel (per-tab state)
  historyPanelOpenTabs: {},
  historyPanelWidth: (() => {
    try {
      const saved = localStorage.getItem('noted-terminal-history-panel-width');
      return saved ? Math.max(280, Math.min(700, parseInt(saved, 10))) : 580;
    } catch { return 580; }
  })(),
  historyScrollToUuid: null,
  setHistoryPanelOpen: (tabId, open) => set(state => ({
    historyPanelOpenTabs: { ...state.historyPanelOpenTabs, [tabId]: open }
  })),
  setHistoryScrollToUuid: (uuid) => set({ historyScrollToUuid: uuid }),

```diff
-   // Reset expansion when tooltip target changes
  useEffect(() => {
    setIsExpanded(false);
  }, [activeTooltipIndex]);

  // Load timeline and fork markers when sessionId changes
+   // Reset expansion when tooltip target changes
  useEffect(() => {
    setIsExpanded(false);
  }, [activeTooltipIndex]);

  // CMD key tracking — tooltip only appears when CMD is held
  useEffect(() => {
    const handleKeyDown = (e: KeyboardEvent) => {
      if (e.key === 'Meta') {
        isCmdHeldRef.current = true;
        setIsCmdHeld(true);
      }
    };
    const handleKeyUp = (e: KeyboardEvent) => {
      if (e.key === 'Meta') {
        isCmdHeldRef.current = false;
        setIsCmdHeld(false);
      }
    };
    const handleBlur = () => {
      isCmdHeldRef.current = false;
      setIsCmdHeld(false);
    };
    window.addEventListener('keydown', handleKeyDown);
    window.addEventListener('keyup', handleKeyUp);
    window.addEventListener('blur', handleBlur);
    return () => {
      window.removeEventListener('keydown', handleKeyDown);
      window.removeEventListener('keyup', handleKeyUp);
      window.removeEventListener('blur', handleBlur);
    };
  }, []);

  // Sync tooltip with CMD key state: show when CMD pressed during hover, hide when released
  useEffect(() => {
    if (isCmdHeld && hoveredIndex !== null) {
      setActiveTooltipIndex(hoveredIndex);
    } else if (!isCmdHeld && !isExpanded) {
      setActiveTooltipIndex(null);
    }
  }, [isCmdHeld, hoveredIndex, isExpanded]);

  // Load timeline and fork markers when sessionId changes
```

       window.addEventListener('keyup', handleKeyUp);
       window.addEventListener('blur', handleBlur);
       return () => { /* cleanup */ };

Now I understand the full picture. Let me analyze the user's three requests:

1. **Viewport dash indicator when History panel is open**: Currently, the timeline tracks which messages are visible in the terminal viewport (dots become dashes/lines). When the History panel is open, can we do the same but based on which entries are visible in the History panel's scroll container? This is actually simpler because the History panel uses `data-uuid` attributes on its entries, so we can use IntersectionObserver or scroll position checks without text search.

2. **Red zone should be disabled when History panel is open**: When the history panel is open, all entries are accessible through the panel, so red (unreachable) highlighting should be removed.


3. **Bug: Plan mode and compact markers not highlighted red**: The reachability check is currently skipping compact, continued, and plan-mode entries entirely, but the user expects these separator lines to also turn red when they fall in the unreachable zone.

Looking at how these are rendered, the fork markers and plan-mode boundaries are separate DOM elements inserted between entries without any unreachable styling logic, while compact entries are actual array entries that get skipped from the reachability check on line 278 and never get the unreachable background applied.

The user is clarifying that plan-mode and compact markers should only be highlighted red when they're surrounded by unreachable entries — not at the boundaries where you can still rewind to history. So the logic needs to check whether all entries after a marker are unreachable, not just apply red unconditionally. Так что логика должна быть: компактные записи и маркеры режима плана становятся недостижимыми, если все записи после них недостижимы, или проще — они наследуют состояние недостижимости от соседних записей. Маркеры между записями (форк, режим плана) — это отдельные элементы, которые должны получать красный фон от прилегающих записей.

Теперь нужно решить три задачи пользователя. Первая: когда панель истории открыта, точки на временной шкале должны показывать, какие записи видны в прокручиваемом контейнере панели истории, используя атрибуты `data-uuid`.

Есть два подхода: либо панель истории сообщает видимые UUID в хранилище Zustand через IntersectionObserver, либо временная шкала напрямую запрашивает DOM панели истории. Первый вариант чище — панель истории будет отслеживать видимые элементы и обновлять хранилище, а временная шкала будет читать из него, когда панель открыта.

Вместо Set в Zustand лучше использовать массив строк, чтобы избежать проблем с перерендерингом. Можно просто расширить существующий обработчик прокрутки в HistoryPanel, чтобы он также отправлял видимые UUID в хранилище.

Но нужно оценить сложность реализации. Первый вариант — добавить в store поле для видимых UUID (5 строк), использовать IntersectionObserver в HistoryPanel для отслеживания видимых элементов (15 строк) и обновить Timeline для использования этих UUID вместо текстового поиска (10 строк) — всего около 30 строк, чистое решение без костылей. Второй вариант — позволить Timeline напрямую запрашивать DOM HistoryPanel, но это менее надежно.

```diff
-   // Resize handle
  const handleResizeMouseDown = useCallback((e: React.MouseEvent) => {
+   // Track visible entries for Timeline viewport indicator (UUID-based, no text search)
  useEffect(() => {
    const el = scrollRef.current;
    if (!el || entries.length === 0) {
      setHistoryVisibleUuids(tabId, []);
      return;
    }

    const visibleSet = new Set<string>();
    prevVisibleUuidsRef.current = '';

    const observer = new IntersectionObserver(
      (observed) => {
        for (const oe of observed) {
          const uuid = (oe.target as HTMLElement).dataset.uuid;
          if (!uuid) continue;
          if (oe.isIntersecting) visibleSet.add(uuid);
          else visibleSet.delete(uuid);
        }
        const key = [...visibleSet].sort().join(',');
        if (key !== prevVisibleUuidsRef.current) {
          prevVisibleUuidsRef.current = key;
          setHistoryVisibleUuids(tabId, [...visibleSet]);
        }
      },
      { root: el, threshold: 0.1 }
    );

    el.querySelectorAll('[data-uuid]').forEach(child => observer.observe(child));

    return () => {
      observer.disconnect();
      setHistoryVisibleUuids(tabId, []);
    };
  }, [tabId, entries.length, setHistoryVisibleUuids]);

  // Resize handle
  const handleResizeMouseDown = useCallback((e: React.MouseEvent) => {

-   const isMultiSelect = selectedTabs.length > 1;
+   // Info panel helper — read-only reference showing current parameters
  const renderInfoPanel = (targetRef: React.RefObject<HTMLDivElement | null>, color: 'blue' | 'orange') => {
    if (!targetRef.current) return null;
    const rect = targetRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
    const accent = color === 'blue' ? 'rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.3)' : 'rgba(218, 119, 86, 0.3)';
    const headerColor = color === 'blue' ? '#60a5fa' : '#DA7756';
    return (
      <SettingsPortal>
        <div style={{
          position: 'fixed',
          left: rect.left - 148,
          top: rect.top - 8,
          zIndex: 10000,
          pointerEvents: 'none',
        }}>
          <div style={{
            backgroundColor: 'rgba(26, 26, 26, 0.98)',
            border: `1px solid ${accent}`,
            borderRadius: '6px',
            padding: '6px 10px',
            fontSize: '10px',
            minWidth: '130px',
            backdropFilter: 'blur(12px)',
            boxShadow: `0 8px 24px rgba(0,0,0,0.5)`,
          }}>
            <div style={{ color: headerColor, fontWeight: 600, marginBottom: 4, fontSize: 9, textTransform: 'uppercase' }}>Параметры</div>
            {[
              { label: 'Редактирование', active: includeEditing },
              { label: 'Чтение', active: includeReading },
              { label: 'С начала', active: fromStart },
            ].map(({ label, active }) => (
              <div key={label} style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center', padding: '1px 0', color: '#999' }}>
                <span>{label}</span>
                <span style={{ color: active ? '#4ade80' : '#555', fontSize: 11 }}>{active ? '●' : '○'}</span>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      </SettingsPortal>
    );
  };

  const isMultiSelect = selectedTabs.length > 1;
```

     - Key additions:
     ```typescript
     const setHistoryVisibleUuids = useUIStore((s) => s.setHistoryVisibleUuids);
     const prevVisibleUuidsRef = useRef('');
     
     // Track visible entries for Timeline viewport indicator (UUID-based)
     useEffect(() => {
       const el = scrollRef.current;
       if (!el || entries.length === 0) { setHistoryVisibleUuids(tabId, []); return; }
       const visibleSet = new Set<string>();
       prevVisibleUuidsRef.current = '';
       const observer = new IntersectionObserver(
         (observed) => {
           for (const oe of observed) {
             const uuid = (oe.target as HTMLElement).dataset.uuid;
             if (!uuid) continue;
             if (oe.isIntersecting) visibleSet.add(uuid);
             else visibleSet.delete(uuid);
           }
           const key = [...visibleSet].sort().join(',');
           if (key !== prevVisibleUuidsRef.current) {
             prevVisibleUuidsRef.current = key;
             setHistoryVisibleUuids(tabId, [...visibleSet]);
           }
         },
         { root: el, threshold: 0.1 }
       );
       el.querySelectorAll('[data-uuid]').forEach(child => observer.observe(child));
       return () => { observer.disconnect(); setHistoryVisibleUuids(tabId, []); };
     }, [tabId, entries.length, setHistoryVisibleUuids]);
     ```

-   // Info panel helper — read-only reference showing current parameters
  const renderInfoPanel = (targetRef: React.RefObject<HTMLDivElement | null>, color: 'blue' | 'orange') => {
    if (!targetRef.current) return null;
    const rect = targetRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
    const accent = color === 'blue' ? 'rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.3)' : 'rgba(218, 119, 86, 0.3)';

+   // Info panel helper — read-only reference showing current parameters

  const renderInfoPanel = (blockRef: React.RefObject<HTMLDivElement | null>, color: 'blue' | 'orange') => {
    if (!blockRef.current) return null;
    const blockRect = blockRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
    const accent = color === 'blue' ? 'rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.3)' : 'rgba(218, 119, 86, 0.3)';
    const headerColor = color === 'blue' ? '#60a5fa' : '#DA7756';

    return (

        <div style={{
          position: 'fixed',
          left: blockRect.left - 148,
          top: blockRect.top + blockRect.height / 2 - panelHeight / 2,
          zIndex: 10000,
          pointerEvents: 'none',
        }}>

            backgroundColor: 'rgba(26, 26, 26, 0.98)',

1. **Info panel horizontal alignment** — now uses `blockRef` (the parent container div) instead of `titleRef` for positioning, so both Update Docs (blue) and Copy Session (orange) info panels align flush with the left edge of their respective blocks

3. **Settings icon (📋) moved inside the orange block** — removed the outer `<div className="flex items-center gap-1">` wrapper, moved the icon inside the orange block div. Now the orange background extends to include the icon

4. **Orange block full width** — changed from `flex-1` to `w-full` so it matches the Update Docs block width
